	focus = {
		id = GER_rhineland
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_military_sphere
		x = 18
		y = 0
		cost = 5
		available = {
			date > 1932.12.31
			is_puppet = no
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SAR
			}
		}
		allow_branch = {
			date > 1932.12.31
			date < 1949.1.1
		}
		bypass = {
			42 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			51 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			788 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			789 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			790 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			791 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			792 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				date < 1937.1.1
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			42 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			51 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			788 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			789 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			790 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			791 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			792 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_rhineland_ultimatum
			add_political_power = 120
			army_experience = 5
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 2
				name = GER_rhineland
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						is_puppet = no
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					country_event = {
						id = germany.60
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = may_provoke_hostility
				}
			}
		}
	}
	focus = {
		id = GER_anschluss
		icon = GFX_RON_goal_anschluss_new
		prerequisite = {
			focus = GER_rhineland

								}

					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = industrial_complex
										size > 0
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
